M01.01卍轮王佛顶一字陀罗尼卍
namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  oṃ  bhrūṃ

M01.02卍一切如来部母佛眼陀罗尼卍
namaḥ sarva tathā gate bhyo  rha bhyaḥ  samya ksaṃ buddhe bhyaḥ  oṃ  ruru  sphuru  jvala  tiṣṭha  siddha locani  sarva artha sadhane  svāhā

M01.03 卍白伞盖佛顶真言(大白伞盖佛顶陀罗尼) (白伞盖佛顶陀罗尼)卍
namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  oṃ  tathagatoṣṇīṣa  anavalokita mūrdhna  oṃ  mama mama  hūṃ  ni

M01.04 卍光聚佛顶陀罗尼 (光聚佛顶王陀罗尼)卍
namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  oṃ  tathagatoṣṇīṣa  anavalokite  mūrdha tejuraśi  oṃ  jvala jvala  dhaka dhaka  vidhaka vidhaka  dara dara  vidara vidara  cchinda cchinda  bhinda bhinda  hūṃ hūṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  svāhā

M01.05 卍高佛顶王陀罗尼卍
namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  oṃ  jvala jvala  dīpya dīpya  dīpyo dgato ṣṇīṣa  dhuna dhuna  hūṃ

M01.06 卍胜佛顶王陀罗尼卍
namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  oṃ  jvala jayo ṣṇīṣa  jvala jvala   bandha bandha dama dama  drūṃ drūṃ drūṃ  haḥ hana  hūṃ

M01.07 卍办事真言(一切佛顶心真言)(办事佛顶陀罗尼)卍
namo bhagavato ṣṇīṣāya  oṃ  ṭrūṃ bandha svāhā

M01.08 卍摧坏真言(摧坏大明王佛顶真言)(摧坏佛顶陀罗尼)卍
namo bhagavato ṣṇīṣāya  oṃ  vikiraṇa  dhuna dhuna  dhūḥ

M01.09 卍摧毁佛顶真言(摧毁佛顶陀罗尼)卍
namo bhagavato ṣṇīṣāya  sarva vighna  vidhvaṃsana karāya  ṭroṭaya  svāhā

M01.10 卍无能胜佛顶真言(无能胜佛陀罗尼)卍
namo bhagavato ṣṇīṣāya  sarvatra aparājitāya  oṃ  śamaya śamaya  śānte dānte  dharmarāja bhaṣite  mahā vidya  sarva artha sadhane   svāhā

M01.11 卍遍照佛顶陀罗尼卍
namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  āḥ maḥ haṃ

M01.12 卍轮王佛顶心陀罗尼卍
namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  apratihata  śasanānāṃ  oṃ  tathā gatoṣṇīṣa  anavalokita mūrdhne  cakravarti  hūṃ  jvala jvala  dhaka dhaka  dhuna vidhuna  trāsaya  mālayotsadaya  hana hana  bhañja bhañja  aṃ aṃ  aḥ aḥ  kaḥ kaḥ  pruṃkhini pruṃkhini  kuṇḍalini  aparājita  stradhariṇi  hūṃ hūṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  svāhā

M01.14 卍如来钵陀罗尼卍

M01.16卍轮王佛顶祈雨陀罗尼卍

M01.17卍轮王佛顶止雨陀罗尼卍

M01.18卍轮王佛顶止非时恶风雨雹陀罗尼卍
saṃrundhami  vāsukī prasukhā nāgā rājānū  ye manu ṣyānāṃ  saṃsyaṃ vihe ṭhayanti  namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  bhrūṃ  catu rdikṣu nāgānāṃ  praviśa asmiṃ kumbhe  sarva duṣṭa nāgānāṃ  ruddhami  svāhā

M01.19卍光聚佛顶烧萎花白芥子止雨陀罗尼卍
namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  apratihata  śāsanānāṃ  oṃ  tathā gato ṣṇīṣa  anavalokita mūrdha tejoraśi  hūṃ  jvala jvala  dhaka dhaka  vidhaka vidhaka  dara dara  vidara vidara  cchinda cchinda  bhinda bhinda  hūṃ hūṃ  sarva duṣṭa nāga varṣā stambhaya  sphaṭ sphaṭ  svāhā

M02.02 卍大佛顶心陀罗尼(亦名小佛顶)卍
namaḥ sarva buddha bodhi satve bhyaḥ  namo ratna trayāya  namaḥ stathā gatāyā rhate samya ksaṃ buddhāya  tasmai nama skṛtvenāṃ  bhagavata stathā gato ṣṇīṣaṃ  sarva deveḥ nama skṛtaṃ  sarva deveḥ pūjitaṃ  sarva deveḥśca paripālitaṃ  sarva bhūta graha nigraha karaṃ  durdantānāṃ  satvānaṃ damakaṃ  duṣṭanaṃ  nivarakaṃ  tadyathā  oṃ  bho bho jvalita  vajrapaṇi  praviśapraviśenaṃ  bhagavata sathā gato ṣṇīṣaṃ  yatsatyaṃ yadbhūtaṃ  tena satyena  tena samayena  udruha udruha  haha haha  matha matha  paramantrāṃ  rakṣa rakṣā atma mantrā  yadyapita tathā gata samaya kṛtaṃ  mantrāṃ  sarvāṃ  cchinda cchinda  bhinda bhinda  paroruha  oṃ trūṃ  oṃ  jambhana  oṃ trūṃ  stambhana  oṃ trūṃ  mohana  oṃ trūṃ  mathana  oṃ trūṃ  bandhana  oṃ trūṃ  rakṣa mama 称名sarva satvā nāṃca  bhagavaṃ stathā gatoṣṇīṣaṃ  namo stute  sita darśana  jvalitānala arka  prabha sphuṭa  vika sitatta patra  jvala jvala  dara dara  vidara vidara  hūṃ hūṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  hehe phaṭ  amogha phaṭ  apratihata phaṭ  varada phaṭ  varaprada phaṭ  sura asura vidrā paka phaṭ  rakṣa rakṣa māṃ  yekecitsatva duṣta cittā  pāpacitta  raudracittā  utpā dayanti  kīlayanti  vidveṣa yanti  moha yanti  mantra yanti  japanti  juhvanti  teṣāṃ pañca yojana  śatābhya ntareṇa  sīma bandha ṅkaromi  vidyā bandha ṅkaromi  tejo bandha ṅkaromi  hasta bandha ṅkaromi  pāda bandha ṅkaromi  sarvaṅga pratyaṅga bandha ṅkaromi  tadyathā  oṃ  anala anala  viśada viśada  vaira vajra dhara  bandha bandha bandhani  vajrapāṇi  hūṃ hūṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  svāhā

oṃ  mahā vajro ṣṇīṣa  hūṃ  traḥ  hrīḥ  aḥ  hūṃ

namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  apratihata  śāsanānāṃ  oṃ  kha kha  khāhi khāhi  hūṃ hūṃ  jvala jvala  prajvala prajvala  tiṣṭha tiṣṭha  ṣṭrī  sphaṭ sphaṭ  svāhā

M02.05 卍大力佛顶陀罗尼卍
namaḥ sarva buddha bodhi satve bhyaḥ  namaḥ stathā gato ṣṇīṣaya  bhagavate  sarvatra aprati hātāya  mahā bodhi satva nama skṛtāya  atibalāya  mahā balāya  mahā vikramāya  sarva devada ndanāya  sahasra surya dīptāya  varāṅgāya  varadāya  sarva satva pūjita nama skṛtāya  sarva deva asura banditāya  mahā maṇi śata dīpti dharāya  amita puṇya koṭīśata virājitāya  aneka lakṣaṇa śata prati maṇḍiṃ tāya  mahā raśmi jvala maṇḍala  vini ścaritā vabhā sita  vigatā ndha kārāya  mahā prativyaṃ vāya  pratimaya  tadyathā  oṃ  namo stute  mahā guṇa  koṭīguṇa  kiraṇa guṇa  maṇi dharāya  hala hala  hārāṃ vara dhara  prati ṣṭhāna śāsana  parama parama  vara vara  varāṅga veṣa dhara  praṇata sasura asura  nama skṛta caraṇa  hulu hulu  maṇḍita kṣaṇḍa  tsaṭṭa tsaṭṭa  vitsaṭṭa vitsaṭṭa  gaṇa gaṇa  guṇa guṇa  gaṇṇa gaṇṇa  ḍhaṇṇa ḍhaṇṇa  bhaṭa bhaṭa  ḍhaṭa ḍhaṭa  bhāṭa bhāṭa  hiḍi hiḍi  mahā locana  virocana  samanta locana  mahā kāruṇika  śubhajñāna prati maṇḍita śarīra  vara vara  vīra vīra  vigata  tamundhakāra  vigatā varaṇa  vigata śoka  vigata mala  vīra viraja  śāsana  namo stute  mahā sagarāya  svāhā  merāvai  svāhā  mahā vimānāya  svāhā  dīptāya  svāhā  pradīptāya  svāhā  pratimaṇḍitāya  svāhā  virājitāya  svāhā  banditāya  svāhā  pūjitāya  svāhā  nama skṛtāya  svāhā  satkṛtāya  svāhā  guru kṛtāya  svāhā  mānitāya  svāhā  anantā nityā dīptaye  svāhā  tejo maṇḍalāya  svāhā  mahā maṇḍalāya  svāhā  apratihata śāsanāya  svāhā  mahā sura samara vijayāya  svāhā  indra  mahīndra  dhanada  varuṇa  maheśvara narayaṇa  nama skṛtāya  svāhā  namaḥ svasti  svāhā  sarva jina vare bhyaḥ  svāhā  namo stute  svāhā

M03.01卍尊胜佛顶陀罗尼(佛顶尊胜陀罗尼)卍
namo bhagavate  trailokya  prati viśi ṣṭhāya  buddhāya  bhagavate  tadyathā  oṃ  viśodhaya  sama samanta  vabhasa spharaṇa  gati gahana  svabhāva śuddhe  abhiṣiñca māṃ  sugata  vara vācana  amṛtābhiṣekeḥ   āhara āhara  āyuḥ sandhāraṇi  śodhaya śodhaya  gagana viśuddhe  uṣṇīṣa vijaya viśuddhe  sahasra raśmi sañcodite  sarva tathā gata  adhiṣṭhā nādhiṣṭhita  mudre  vajrakāya  saṅha tana śuddhe  sarva āvaraṇā viśuddhe  prati nivarttāya āyuḥ śuddhe  samayā dhiṣṭhite  maṇi maṇi  tathatā bhuta koṭi pari śuddhe  visphuṭa buddhi śuddhe  jaya jaya  vijaya vijaya   smara  smara  sarva buddhā dhiṣṭhita śuddhe  vajre vajra garbhe  vajraṃ bhavatu mama 称名 sarva satvā nāṃca kāya viśuddhe  sarva gati pari śuddhe  sarva tathā gata samā śvāsā  dhiṣṭite  buddhya buddhya  bodhaya bodhaya  samanta pariśuddhe  sarva tathā gata  adhiṣṭhā nādhiṣṭhita  mahā mudre  svāhā

M03.04 卍别译尊胜佛顶陀罗尼卍
namo bhagavate  trailokya  prati viśiṣṭāya  buddhāya  bhagavate  tadyathā  oṃ  viśo dhaya viśodhaya  samā sama samanta  vabhasa spharaṇa  gati gahana  svabhāva viśuddhe  abhiṣiñcatu maṃ  sugata  vara vācana  amṛta bhiṣekeḥ  āhara āhara  āyuḥ sandhāraṇi  śodhaya śodhaya  gagana viśuddhe  uṣṇīṣa vijaya viśuddhe  sahasra raśmi sañcodite  sarva tathā gatā  valokani  ṣaṭpāra mita pari pūraṇi  sarva tathā gata  hṛdayā  dhiṣṭhā nadhiṣṭhita  mahā mudre  vajrakāya  saṇha tana viśuddhe  sarva avaraṇā  pāya durgati pari śuddhe  prati niva rttāya āyuḥ śuddhe  samaya adhiṣṭhite  mani mani  mahā mani  tatha ttā bhuta  koṭi pari śuddhe  visphuṭa buddhi śuddhe  jaya jaya  vijaya vijaya   smara  smara  sarva buddhā dhiṣṭhita śuddhe  vajre vajra garbhe  vajraṃ bhavatu mama称名  śarīraṃ  sarva satvānāṃca kāya pari śuddhe  sarva gati pari śuddhe  sarva tathā gata ścame  samā śvasayantu  sarva tathā gata  samā śvāsā dhiṣṭhite  buddhya buddhya  vibodhaya vibodhaya  samanta pari śuddhe  sarva tathā gata hṛdayā  dhiṣṭhā nādhiṣṭhita  mahā mudre   svāhā

M03.06卍诸佛心陀罗尼卍
tadyathā  buddhe subuddhe  mahā buddhe  iti buddhe  tatra buddhe  buddhe buddhe  sama buddhe  abhibuddhe  mūrdhna buddhe  buddha mati buddhe  mahā buddha mati buddhe  sarva buddha anumate  sarva buddha anujate  buddha buddha buddha buddha buddha buddha buddha buddha buddha buddha ananto buddha viṣaya  ananta dharmma deśanāḥ  ekanta mana sikāra  saṅkṣipta dharmma bhavanā  ittāni sarva buddhe  bhidhāraṇi  saṃ prakā śitā  anukampāya  satvānāṃ  sarva dharmmānāṃ mudrāṇī  tadyathā  śuddhe suśuddhe  śodhane  śodhane  nirmale  malāpagate  gati sa matikrānte  krama krama sāgare  sāgarapati  sukke visukke  śoka śamane  śānte upaśante  praśa ntāva bhase  sarva buddha pratimaṇḍite  sarva puṇya parimaṇḍite  sarva dharmma prati maṇḍite  hara hara  maraṃ hara  cara cara  sañcara  cala cala  sañcala  tala tala  santala  sama tala  nire nire sunire  hṛda mati  loka dhare  loka dhā raṇi  dhara dhara  ṭhara ṭhara  krodha krodha mahā vijaya vāhini  hara hara  sarva buddho preṣitasi  sarva jñāpathe  sarva prajñā para mite  mahā pratibhāna sapanne  samanta loke  buddha viṣaye  buddha prati maṇḍite  bhagavati  sara sara  prasara prasara  visara visara  sarva doṣāpagate  svāhā

M03.07卍诸佛心能令一切众生安乐陀罗尼卍
namaḥ sarva tathā gate bhyo  rha bhyaḥ  samyaksaṃ buddhe bhyaḥ  tadyathā  jaya jaya  jaya vaha  cili cili  miri mili  luṭu luṭu  jaye vijaye  vijayanti  ajite  aparajite  sarva duṣṭa praduṣṭa  stambhani  jambhani  mohani  śvete karāre  keyūre  sarva buddhā dhiṣṭhite  paṇḍara vāsini  parṇa śavari  śriye  mahaśriye  sarvā tyodaya śriye  padma vahe  padma mālini  vajra ṅkuśi  vajra mate śolini  cakra dhare  hihi vajra paṇi  hehe vajra paṇi  hihi hihi  hehe hehe  vajra paṇi  hihi hehe  vajra paṇi  kara kara  rala rala  bala bala  dhama dhama  sara sara  hāhā hāhā  cile cile  cchile dile  didile  mimile  jvale  mahā jvale  jvalite  prajva lite  ikkudhara  dhākke ṭhale  mukuṭe kṣeme  kṣamame  siddha saṅgha nama skṛte  sarva deva hṛdaya vartini  sarva satvā hṛdaya jayanti vartini  sarva satvā hṛdaya bodhani  sarva duṣṭa praduṣṭa hṛdaya mathani  sarva tathā gata hṛdayanupālane  sarva bodhi satva hṛdaya vaiśani  ehyehi  samaya manu palaya  sarva satvānāṃ hṛdaya dyāka rṣayeca  sthāpaya  namaḥ sarva vide  svāhā  loka vide  svāhā  traṭa traṭa  sphoṭaya sphoṭaya  svāhā  ulokanīye  svāhā  mahā karīye  svāhā  vilokanīye  svāhā  mahā karīye  svāhā  agnaye  svāhā  brahmaṇe  svāhā  viṣṇave  svāhā  rudrebhya  svāhā  śakrāya  svāhā  lokapālebhya  svāhā  viśvebhyo devebhya  svāhā  vasubhya  svāhā  mātṛbhya  svāhā  sarva vighna vinā yake bhya  svāhā  pṛthivye  svāhā  sara srātye  svāhā  sarva deva  nāga  yakṣa  gandharva  asura  garuḍa  kinnara  mahoraga  yakṣa rakṣasa  prabhṛti bhyaḥ  sarva traidha ttuka paryā panne bhyaḥ  sarva satve bhyaḥ  svāhā  ehyehi  āgaccha āgaccha  samaya manu pālaya  kuru kuru  sara sara  tiṣṭha tiṣṭha  hana hana  daha daha  paca paca  huṃ  yuṃ  puṃ  caṇḍāya mataṅgi  brahmāṇi pukkasi  namaḥ sarva tathā gate bhyaḥ  siddhyantu mantra padā  svāhā

M03.15卍佛心陀罗尼卍
namo bhagavato  tītānāgata pratyu tpannānāṃ  samya ksaṃ buddhānāṃ  saśrā vaka saṅghānāṃ  namo maitreya pramukhānāṃ  bodhi satvānāṃ  athāto buddha hṛdayaṃ  avartta iṣyāmi  tadyathā  hili hili  mili mili  kili kili  kirali kirali  bhagavāṃ  buddha buddha hini hini  bodhaya bodhaya  bhagavāṃ buddha maitreṇa  hara hara  kamari kamari  śaṅkari śaṅkari  mari mari  śabhi śabhi  śavari śavari  saṃbodhaya  bhagavāṃ buddhamai treṇa  cara cara  śīghraṃ śīghraṃ  curu curu  muru muru  murāpaya  mārasaidyaṃ vidrāpaya  dhari dhari  viri viri  bhagavāṃ cūḍamaṇi  śīghraṃ śīghraṃ  para para  lāmudari  giri giri  hana hana  kiri kiri  vege vege  turu turu  saṃbodhaya  bhagavāṃ buddha maitreṇa  kala kala  mala mala  hāhāhāhā hāhāhā  gavidrāpaṇa  hasa hasa  muñcāṭṭa hāsa  sphoṭaya  nāga giri bhavanāṃ  kampāpaya  trāsaya  saṃmohaya  bhrāmaya bhrāmaya  hiri hiri  bhagavāṃ buddha maitreṇa  hehe hehe  hṛdaya manu smarāhi  jaya jaya  dhāva dhāva  hṛdayaṃ  gṛhṇa gṛhṇa  hiri hiri  hiri hiri  kiri kiri  bhagavāṃ buddha maitreṇa  huṃ huṃ huṃ huṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  nāśaya nāśaya  caṇḍa caṇḍa  tara tara  tāri tāri  tāraya tāraya  hara hara  tara vīre  hara hara  matta mayūrī  tara vīre  moraya moraya  tiri tiri  dhāriṇi dhāriṇi  tara vīre  caṇḍi caṇḍi  daṇḍi daṇḍi  dara dara  daṇḍa vīre  javi javi  paca paca  tīre tīre  aparājitotare  māra sainya vidrapanī  miri miri  dimi dimi  dhasi dhasi  kaṃ malā śvatare  vege vege  smarāhi  bhagavāṃ buddha maitreṇa  yastvahi bodhimūle  vajropama samdhi  samāghando  taṃ bhagavāṃ hṛdaya  manu smara  bodhaya bodhaya  jayanti jayanti  kāri kāri  kīkāri kīkāri  kiri kiri  kiṅkari kiṅkari  dhāva dhāva  kili kili  kampa kampa  kampā paya   smara bhagavāṃ  jayotarā  nāma vidyā  svāhā  sarva artha siddhāya  svāhā  sabuddhāya  svāhā  sarva jñāya  svāhā  sarva dharme śvarāya  svāhā  anindāya  svāhā  aninda guṇāya  svāhā  aninda vimalāya  svāhā  sarva satva kāruṇikāya  svāhā  apratihata śāsanāya  svāhā

M03.16卍金刚手说佛心陀罗尼(佛心陀罗尼)卍
namo bhagavato vajra paṇaye  guhya kādhi pataye  tadyathā  hihi vajrapaṇi  hehe vajra paṇi  hī hī vajrapaṇi  kili kili vajra paṇi  kuru kuru śabdena  dhara dhara  kili kili  hana hana vajreṇa  hihi hihi  hini hini  rāva rāva  nīlamvaradhara vajrapaṇi  hiri hiri  kiri kiri  vajravajra vajravajra  vajrāṭṭahasa  kuru kuru  kulu kulu  kumbhaṇḍāṃ trasaya vajreṇa  martha martha  udālaya vajreṇa  vajrakāla kalaṃ  para para  huṃ huṃ huṃ huṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  trāsaya vajreṇa  hana hana  kaḍha kaḍha  trasaya vajreṇa  matha matha bhramaya  kara kara  laghu laghu  kākā kīkī  kuru kuru  bhagavaṃ vajra kāla  para para  hana hana  kulutsādanaṃ  kuru kuru  kṛṣṇa śavara piśacā dhi pataye  ehi miri vajra  miri kiri vajra  kiri tiri vajra  tiri viri vajra  viri śavari vajra  śavara varma vajra  ībhū nirbhū tabhū  miri mari  kṛṣṇa śavara śavari piśacā dhipataye  kuru kuru guhya kādhi pataye  piri piri caṇḍa vajrakāla  divyakanana  rājata vajra vaiḍūrya  mukti kāñcanā laṅkṛtā bharaṇa  bhaṇḍa bhaṇḍa  gaccha gaccha  nivedaya  śīghraṃ vajracihna  laghu laghu  jalpāpaya kelapaya  kampapaya  kiṭi moṭapaya  raṅgāpaya  trasaya  samohaya  bhramaya bhramaya vajreṇa  vajracaṇḍa  caṇḍa graha  ākuṭaya ākāśaṃ stambhaya  divyaṃ stambhaya  nāgagrahaṇa  yakṣa grahaṇa  sarva duṣṭa grahaṇāṃ  paca pācaya  stambhaya  bandha bandha ciri ciri  bhara bhara  pūra pūra  pūrapaya vajreṇa  apasmāra grahaṃ āveśaya  cara cara  para para  pūrapaya pūrapaya vajreṇa  vighnaṃ hana hana  vitrāsaya  akaḍha akaḍha  vajrā kuśena  dhiri dhiri  skandha grahaṃ utsadaya  bhagavāṃ vajrapaṇi  karmame kuru kuru  muru muru  huru huru  ārya siddha ścaṇḍa vajrapaṇi rājña payati  svāhā

M08.13卍随求大护明王陀罗尼(随求大护明王大心陀罗尼)卍

M08.14卍毗婆尸佛陀罗尼(七佛世尊毗婆尸佛陀罗尼)卍

M08.15卍尸弃佛陀罗尼(尸弃佛在空中欲为一切众生除一切病故欲除一切恶鬼障难故而说陀罗尼)卍

M08.21卍虚空藏菩萨陀罗尼(尒时虚空藏菩萨摩诃萨亦说护持一切 无量众生除一切障罪业殃一切恶鬼一切病故说此陀罗尼)卍

M09.01 卍无垢净光根本陀罗尼(最胜无垢清净光明根本陀罗尼)卍
namaḥ sapta saptatti bhyaḥ  samya ksaṃ buddhā koṭīnāṃ   pari śuddha kāyavāki citta  prati ṣṭhitānāṃ  namo bhagavate  amitā yuṣasya tathā gatasya  oṃ  tathā gata śuddhe  āyuḥ viśodhani  saṅhara saṅhara  sarva tathā gata vīrya balena  prati saṅhara āyu   smara  smara  sarva tathā gata samayaṃ  bodhi bodhi  buddhya vibuddhya  bodhaya bodhaya  sarva satvānāṃ  sarva papa avaraṇa viśuddhe  vigata mala mala bhaye  subuddha buddhe  huru huru  svāhā

M09.02 卍相轮橖中陀罗尼卍
oṃ  sarva tathā gata vipula yaṣṭi  maṇi kanaka rājāta  vibhuṣita yaṣṭi dhuru dhuru  samanta vilokite  sara sara  sarva papa viśodhane  bodhani  saṃbodhani  pravara yaṣṭhi  vare maṇi dhvaje  rucira mala viśuddhe  hūṃ hūṃ  svāhā

M09.03 卍修造塔陀罗尼卍

M09.04 卍除盖障菩萨说一切佛心陀罗尼卍
namo bhagavataṃ navānavatīnāṃ  samya ksaṃ buddha koṭīna yuta  śatasahasra  gaṅgāna dīvaluka samānāṃ namaḥ sarva nīvaraṇa viṣkambhiṇi bodhi satvāya  oṃ  turu turu  sarvā varaṇa viśodhani  sarva tathā gata āyuḥ pālani  vipule  nirmale  sarva siddha nama skṛte  bhara bhara  sarva satvā valokini  hūṃ  sarva nīvaraṇa viṣkambhiṇi  sarva pāpa viśodhani  svāhā

M09.05卍轮橖及塔四周陀罗尼卍

M09.06 卍相轮中及旋遶陀罗尼卍

 M10.02 卍曼殊室利菩萨千钵陀罗尼(金刚界大神变千钵圣曼殊室利童真大菩萨一百八名陀罗尼)(千臂千鉢曼殊室利菩萨金刚三摩地祕密根本菩提真言)卍

namo sarva jñāya  namo ratna trayāya  namo amitābhaya tathā gatāyā  rhate samya ksaṃ buddhāya  namaḥ āryā valokite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  mahā kāruṇikāya  namo mahā sthāmapraptāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  mahā kāruṇikāya  namo vipula vimāna  supratiṣṭhita  saṅkheya surya  śatasahasrātireka  prabhavabhasita mūrttaye  mahā maṇi mukuṭa kuṇḍala dhariṇi  bhagavati  mahā padmapāṇaye  sarva lokāpāya  śamanāya  vividha duḥkha samāvaiśāviṣṭa  sarva satvā parimocanāya  tadyathā  oṃ  bhūrbhuvaḥ  mahā lokākaraṇa  tama stimira  vajra paṭṭala  vināśana karāya  raga dveṣa moha jāla śamaka  śāsaka rakṣaka  sarvāpāya duḥkha durgati  praśamana karāya  sarva tathā gata sama vardhana kara  sarva satvāśāpari pūraka  sarva satva samaśvasa kara  ehyehi  mahā bodhi satva varada  padma loka saṃbhūta  mahā kāruṇika  jaṭāmakuṭā  laṅkṛta  śiru maṇi kanaka rājata  vajravaiḍūrya  laṅkṛta śarīra  amitābhajina  kamala mālālaṅkṛta  pravara nara narī  mahā jana naradāri  śatasahasra abhilāṣitakāya  mahā bodhi satva  vidhama vidhama  vināśaya vināśaya  mahā yantru kleśaka  vāṭāva  vardha sāṃsāracāraka  pramathana  puruṣapadma  puruṣanaga  puruṣasa gara  vīraja viraja  sudanta sudanta  parivṛta  dhama dhama  sama sama  dhuru dhuru  praśāsaya praśasaya  ghiri ghiri  viri viri  ciri ciri  curu curu  muru muru  muyu muyu  muñca muñca  bhagavaṃ  āryāvalokiteśvara  rakṣa rakṣa mama 称名  sarva satvānāṃca  sarva bhaye bhyaḥ  dhuna dhuna  vidhuna vidhuna  dhuru dhuru  gaya gaya  gadhaya gadhaya  hasa hasa  prahasa prahasa  vividha kleśavasana  mama  sarva satvānāṃca  hara hara  saṅhara saṅhara  dhuruṭi dhuruṭi  mahā maṇḍala karaṇa  śata praseka vabhasa  viṣaṇa śamaka  mahā bodhi satva varada  svāhā

M16.03卍奋怒王真言(不空奋怒王陀罗尼)(最上不空奋怒王陀罗尼)卍
namaḥ sarva tathā gata  āryā valokite śvara  vajra dhare bhyaḥ  oṃ  cara cara  ciri ciri  curu curu  mahā kāru ṇika  ciri ciri  viri viri  mahā padma hasta  kala kala  kili kili  kulu kulu  mahā sthāma prapta  cara cara  cacara  niśacare śvara  ehyehi  siddhya siddhya  buddhya buddhya  dhava dhava  kiṇi kiṇi  parama śuddha satva  kara kara  kiri kiri  kuru kuru  mahā paśu pati veṣa dhara  hāhā hīhī hūhū  oṃ kara  brahma veṣa dhara  sara sara  vara vara  raśmi śata saha sra  pratima ṇḍita śarīra  jvala jvala  tapa tapa  bhagavaṃ  suma nitya yama varuṇa kuvera  brahmi ndra  iṛṣi deva gaṇa  bhya rcitta caraṇa  suru suru  muru muru  sana tku māra  rudra vasava  dhanada  deva iṛṣi nāyaka  bahu vivi dha veṣa dhara  dhara dhara  samantā valokita  vilokita loke śvara  mahe śvara  muyu muyu  muñca muñca  vadha bandhana  taḍana rājata skara  āgnyu daka  viṣa śastra  parimo caka  kaṇa kaṇa  bala bodhi ṅga  catu ārya satya  saṃ praka śaka  tama tama  sama sama  masa masa  mahā vidya ndhakara  praśamana  mili mili  eṇeya carma pari kara  ehyehi  maṭa maṭa  viśuddha viṣaya vasiṃ  mahā kāru ṇika  śveta yajṇo pavīta  ratna makuṭa mala dhara  sarva jña śirasi  kṛta kara puṭa  dhyāna sama dhi  vimo kṣa prakaṃ pya  ṣa ṭpara mita  pari pū raka  bahu satva santati  paripā caka  sarva mārani duṣṭa  pramardaka  sarva siddhyā śāpari pūraka  abhi ṣi ñca  sarva tathā gatā bhiṣeke  bhagavaṃ amogha rāja  hūṃ  phaṭ  namo stute  svāhā

M16.04卍悉地王真言(不空悉地王陀罗尼)卍
namo ratna trayāya  namaḥ ārya amitā bhāya tathā gatāya  namaḥ āryā valokite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  mahā kāru ṇikāya  tadyathā  oṃ  padme padme  padma dhara vibhu ṣita bhuje  cara cara  brahma veṣa dhara  bhara bhara  vicitra mauli dhara  maṇi kanaka  vajra vaiṇū ryā laṅkṛta śarīra  tara tara  taraya bhagavaṃ  bhagavati paraṃ  dhuru dhuru  amogha paśa hasta  vara vara  vara dayaka  samantā valokita  mahā bodhi satva varada  padma sāna  padma gaura  jvala jvala  sarva tathā gatā bhi ṣekā bhi ṣikta  mahā kāru ṇika  bala bala  mahā bala vega dhara  vikṛta nāna  daṃ ṣṭrā karala  mahā teja dhara  vipula jñana varada  mahā kāru ṇika  mahā paśu pati veṣa dhara  sara sara  prasara  puṇya saṃ bhara  sugata dhyana sama dhi  samantā valokita  īśvara  mahe śvara  duṣṭa damaka  raudra pralaya  damaka krodharāja  mahā vega dhara  sama sama  mahā sthāma prapta  candra sūrya  trika prabha  mala mala  sarva mala viśo dhaka  sarva iṛṣi gaṇa santati  mahā mahe śvara rūpa dhara  amitā bhaji nālaṅkṛta  jaṭā dakṣiṇa  candra laṅkṛta śira  matha matha  sarva yakṣa rakṣasa  bhūta gaṇa bhañjaka  tara tara  tara gaṇa samalaṅkṛta  dakṣa tra mara  sarva vighna vinā śana kara  parama maitra citta  mahā kāru ṇika  para para  pari pūrṇa maṇḍala  sau mya mukha  ṣa ṭpāra mita pari pūraka  miri miri  eṇeya carma  vasāna vya ghra carmo tarya  dhara dhara  sarva tathā gatā valokita  trine tra  triśula dhara  vajra jvala dhara  amogha pāśa hasta  yama varuṇa  kuvera rūpa dhara  nagi ndra rūpa dhara  vimala viśo dhaneha  sarva papa praśamaka  sarvā varaṇa viśo dhaka  sarva kilviṣa naśaka  tre lokya vaśaṅkara  sarva satva viśo dhaka  bodhi bodhi  bodhi satva varada  sarva tathā gatā dhiṣṭhite  oṃ  padma vibhu ṣita śuddhe  dhiri dhiri  āva lokaya māṃ  sama sama  sarva karma vesā dhaya  amogha paśa hṛdaya  siddhe guhya  deva sini  varada  hūṃ  phaṭ  namo stute  svāhā

M16.05卍吉祥莲花真言(吉祥莲花陀罗尼)卍
namo ratna trayāya  namaḥ āryā valokite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  mahā kāru ṇikāya  mahā moghā vara dāya  tadyathā  oṃ  padmini  padmini tripa dmo ṅge  padma dhare  padma vati  padma priye  padma gauri  padma prabhe  padma sāna  prati ṣṭhite  ava lokita priye  varade varada yini  prasina prasi naya  kuru kuru  āryā valokite śvara varade  huru huru  vara dā ṅgini  cala cala  puṣpa vibhu ṣita  padma priye  vicitra vimāna dhare  bhara bhara  saṃ bhara saṃ bhara   smara  smara  samayaṃ  āryā valokite śvarāya  samaye satyā dhiṣṭhita nime  amogha paśa varade  hūṃ  namo stute  svāhā

M16.06卍功德天与一切愿真言(大吉祥天与一切愿陀罗尼)卍

M16.11卍普遍心印真言(普遍心印陀罗尼)(溥遍心印陀罗尼)卍
namaḥ streya  dhvikānāṃ  tathā gatānāṃ  oṃ  amogha padma paśa krudha aka rṣāya  veśaya  mahā paśu pati  yama varuṇa  kuvera  brahma veṣa dhara  amogha hṛdaya  padma kula  sama yāya  hūṃ hūṃ hūṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  svāhā

M17.01卍不思议观陀罗尼真言卍
nama strya dhva nugata  prati ṣṭhite bhyaḥ  sarva tathā gate bhyaḥ  namaḥ sarva pratyeka buddhā  rya śravaka saṅghe bhyaḥ  namo mai treya pramu khe bhyāḥ  mahā bodhi satva gaṇa vare bhyaḥ  namaḥ ārya vajra dhara  mahā maṇḍala devate bhyaḥ  yama varuṇa kuvera  iṛṣi gaṇa vare bhyaḥ  namo ratna trayāya  namaḥ āryā valokite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  mahā kāru ṇikāya  tadyathā  oṃ  sarva tathā gatā valokita  paśahṛdaya  jvala jvala  dharmma dhātu garbha  cala cala  mahā padma bhuja  dhara dhara  mahā paśadhara  vara vara  raśmi śata saha sra  pratima ṇḍita śarīra  tara tara  vipula teja dhara  bhara bhara  ṣa ṭpāra mita paripū raṇa  kala kala  mahā brahma veṣa dhara  mala mala  sarva papā varaṇa mala  kilviṣa naśana  dhuru dhuru  bodhi satva viśu ddha bhuru bhuru  mahā satva vasala  yama varuṇa kuvera  nama skṛta  huru huru  brahma viṣṇu mahe śvara  kumāra nandike śvara  īśvara  mahe śvara  deva putra bandita  nama skṛta  vividhamaṇi moli dhara  amitā bha jina  makuṭa dhara divya  maṇi kanaka  vajra vai ṇū rya  mara kata  padma ragi ndra nīla  dimya muktika  laṅkṛta śarīra  yajṇo pavīta dhara  jaṭā makuṭa  maṇḍita nava candra  racitta  padma dhara  padma sāna  padma bhuja  trilo cana  tri śula dhara  paśadhara  sarva tathā gatā bhi ṣi kta  sara sara  sarva pāpa praśamana kara  mahā kāru ṇika  turu turu  sarva satva vara dāyaka  bodhi bodhi  sarva tathā gatā valokita  bodhi maṇḍala  valokita  loke śvara  mahe śvara  mahā cinta maṇi dhara  viśva rūpa  mahā sau mya vadhana  mahā kāru ṇika  buddhya buddhya  bodhaya bodhaya  bhagavāṃ  sarva tathā gatā valokita garbha  mahā puṇya teja dhara  pravara siddhi kara  sarva vyā dhi hara  sarva satva naya pāra  sarva duḥkha pramo caka  mahā kāru ṇika  namo stute  svāhā

M17.02卍一切菩萨敬礼解脱三昧耶真言(一切菩萨敬礼解脱三昧耶陀罗尼)卍
nama strya dhva nugata  prati ṣṭhite bhyaḥ  sarva tathā gate bhyaḥ  mahā bodhi satva gaṇa vare bhyaḥ  namaḥ ārya vajra dhara  sarva maṇḍala devata vidyā rāje bhyaḥ  oṃ  amoghā valokita  mahā maṇḍala padme  sarva bodhi satva nama skṛte  bhara bhara  samantā valokite  amogha mahā brahma veṣa dhara  dhara dhara  mahā kāru ṇikā  bodhaya bodhaya  mahā bodhini  padma bodhini  sarva papā ndhakara  praśamani  sarva durgati varaka  mahā kāru ṇika  bahu vivi dhaveṣa dhara  sarva tathā gata garbha  huru huru  amogha garbhe  turu turu  amogha paśahaste  muru muru  vimo kṣa  bhuje  kṣiṇi kṣiṇi  sarva ava raṇa viśuddhe  bhara bhara  sarva tathā gata paripu rate  tara tara  tāraya māṃ  ava lokaya  padma bhuje  maṇi kanaka  vibhu ṣita bahu  dama dama  durda ntanāṃ  mahā bodhi satva varada  mahā kāru ṇika  sarva devata nama skṛta  iṛṣi gaṇa sata mita  śata saha sra  candra sūrya treka  raśmi rava bha sita  mahā paśu pati veṣa dhara  parama śuddhasatva  avalokite śvara  mahe śvara  parama kāru ṇika  mahā maṇḍale śvara  supra buddha mahā padma bhuje śvara  mahā vidyā dhare śvara  dhiri dhiri  mahā dhiri  mahā kāru ṇika  mahā vimo kṣa maṇḍala dhara  sarva tathā gata guhya  mudra samaya dhara  mahā bala vīrya dhara  maṇi moli dhara  amitā bhama kuṭa dhara  dhuru dhuru  samantā valokita  loke śvara  paśadhare śvara  para para  mahā maitrī vilokita  sarva satva sa nta raka  siddhya siddhya  śapa ripū raka  mahā bala prada  namo stute  svāhā  oṃ  dhira dhira  mahā maṇḍala viśva rūpa  ṣa ṭpara mita pari puraka  sarva bodhi satva nama skṛta  parama vipula vimo kṣa dhara  mahā paśavilokita  amogha paśajvalita  mahā jvalā valokita  mahā maṇi dīpta dhara  samanta vabha sita  jvala jvala  mahā ga mbhī ra vimo kṣa paśadhara  bala bodhi ṅga pāka rṣaka  oṃ  brahma rūpa  mahā mogha paśa hūṃ hūṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  sarva satvā valokita  vara prada  namo stute  svāhā

M19.02卍清净莲华明王央俱舍真言(清净莲花明王央俱舍陀罗尼)卍

tadyathā  oṃ  jaye jaye  vijaye vijaye  jayavā hini  śaṅkari śaṅkari  prabhañjani prabhañjani  sarva śatruṇāṃ  jambhaya jambhaya  stambhaya stambhaya  mohaya mohaya  bhagavati  vijaya vāhini  martha martha  prama rtha prama rtha  hasa hasa  grasa grasa  hūṃ hūṃ  la mbo dari la mbo dari  tri netre  catu rmu khe  catu rva ktre  catu rdaṃ ṣṭre  catu rbhuje  asi musala  kha ḍga  triśula  vajra dhariṇi  rakṣa rakṣa māṃ  oṃ  bhagavati  hana hana  daha daha  paca paca  ma rtha ma rtha  prama rtha prama rtha  dhuna dhuna  vidhuna vidhuna  hūṃ hūṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  bhañja bhañja  mara sai nyaṃ  vidhvā ṅsaya  sarva śatrūṃ  dhva jagra keyūre  tṛṭṭa tṛṭṭa  bhṛ ṭṭa bhṛ ṭṭa  u lka dhāriṇi  trai lokya prama rthani  vidhva ṅsaya  māra sai nyaṃ  rakṣa rakṣa māṃ  cala cala  cili cili  culu culu  kala kala  kili kili  kulu kulu  muñcā ṭṭa hasa  vi dhvā ṅsaya  māra sai nyaṃ  bhra maya  buddhasatyena  dharmma satyena  saṅgha satyena  satya vanināṃ satyena  buddhasatyaṃ māti krama  dharmma satyaṃ mati krama  saṅgha satyaṃ mati krama  satya vādināṃ satyaṃ nati krama  vidhvā ṅsaya māra sai nyaṃ  kuṭa kuṭa  kuṭṭa kuṭṭa  rudra mānaya  viṣṇu mānaya  candra sūrya mānaya  devā mānaya  devā dhi pati mānaya  trai lokya adhi pati mānaya  sarva yakṣa rākṣasa  kumbhaṇḍa  garuḍa kinnara maho raga mānaya  rakṣa rakṣa mama sya  vidhvā ṅsaya  māra sai nyaṃ  sarvo pasa rge bhyaḥ  raṅga raṅga  raṅgā paya raṅgā paya  jvala jvala  puṣpa mālini  ciṭṭa ciṭṭa  riṭṭa riṭṭa  tṛ ṭṭa tṛ ṭṭa  bhṛ kuṭī mukhi  māra sai nyaṃ  kulo tsa dana kari  hāhāhā  hīhīhī  hūhūhū  hala hala  hili lili  hulu hulu  he he he  riṇi riṇi  riṇi pati  jaṃ mū dhvaje  buddhā vilokite  sarva tathā gatā vilokite  svāhā  guṇa rāja pra bhase  svāhā  sūryā rka vimale  svāhā  candrā rka vimale  svāhā  sarva grahā nakṣa tra ddhyāmi karaṇe  svāhā  sarvo padra  sarvo pasa rge bhyaḥ  svāhā

M25.01 卍阎曼德迦大威怒王陀罗尼(圣阎曼德迦大威怒王立成大神验陀罗尼)卍

M25.13 卍金刚手大身陀罗尼(金刚手秘密主大身陀罗尼)卍

M26.01 卍甘露军吒利明王成就一切法陀罗尼(圣甘露军吒利明王除一切障难成就一切法陀罗尼)卍

akrama  kiṃ cirā yasi  śīghraṃ śīghraṃ  dhuna dhuna  vidhuna vidhuna  paṭa paṭa  kaṭa kaṭa  kara kara  ghara ghara  para para  pūraya pūraya  gholaya gholaya  curṇaya pātaya  aviśa aviśa śighraṃ M26.14 卍军吒利明王无能胜陀罗尼(甘露军吒利明王无能胜陀罗尼)卍

M26.24 卍军吒利使者陀罗尼(甘露军吒利明王使者陀罗尼)卍
namaḥ sarva buddhānāṃ  namo ratna trayaya  sarva buddhabodhi satve bhyaḥ  ārya mai treya pramu khe bhyaḥ  namaḥ  samya ggate bhyaḥ samya kprati panne bhyaḥ  namo vajra pāṇaye  mahā yakṣa sena pataye  oṃ  amṛta dyuti vajre  huṃ hūṃ  phaṭ  svāhā  tadyathā  oṃ  kaṭa kaṭa  śama śama  śānte śānte  dante dante  dama dama  damane  dhīre dhīre vare  hāme ru dhīre  satye satya bale  hiri hiri  kuṭi kuṭi  ku ṭṭaya ku ṭṭaya  muni muni vare  muni muni  mahā muni  mane mane sumane  sma nase  rakṣa rakṣa mama  nāśaya nāśaya  sarva duṣṭa pradu ṣṭani  teṣā ñca hṛdayani  hara hara  pāpa hṛdayāni  hara hara  haraṇe  prahara praha raṇe  dama damani  paca paca  hana hana  jaha jaha  hūṃ hūṃ  hehe śavari śāvari  mata ṅgi  caṇḍali  hana hana  sarva pratya arthi kāni  śata dhakuru  māsa maya mati krama  bho bho  tiṣṭha tiṣṭha  bandha bandha hasta  pāda  mukhaṃ  gṛva  cakṣo  śro traṃ  hṛdayaṃ  aṅga maṅga  mamāṇi  tāḍaya vajreṇa   smara hṛdayaṃ  mahā mahā bala kāma krodhaṃ  hara hara  ānaya sarva bhutāṇi  bhagavaṃ vajra paṇi  vajra dhara  amṛta vajra krodharāja  vajrā ṭṭa hāsa  na rtta na rtta  kuru kuru  kuñja kuñja  kuha kuha   smara  smara  mahā satva  hohoho  hahaha  haṭina  caṇḍa caṇḍa  mahā caṇḍa  huhu  muru muru  vajreṇa  hana hana  sarva śattroṃ  mama  rakṣa rakṣa  bandha bandha dhāraya  hehe kuru  vajra pāṇi  karma māti krama  samaya  tiṣṭha tiṣṭha  mate tathā gata visaṃ vāṇeto  bhavi ṣyati  namo ratna tryāya  oṃ  amṛta kuṇḍali  huṃ  ānaya dūti  sarva graha dūti  samā jñāpaya  hūṃ hūṃ hūṃ  phaṭ phaṭ phaṭ  svāhā

namaḥ sarva pratyeka buddha śrāvaka bodhi satve bhyaḥ  namo bhagavate  amitā bhaya tathā gatāyā rhate samya ksaṃ buddhāya  namaḥ āryā valokite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  namo mahā sthā mapra ptāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  namaḥ sarva artha siddhāya vidyā rājñī  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  namo mahā śriyāye sarva artha sādhi kāye  bodhi satvāye  sarva vidyā dhara satyena  mahā śriyaṃ prapa dyāmi  deva satyaṃ  indra satyaṃ  vya va hāra satyaṃ  laksa ṇasa tyaṃ  paramā rtha satyaṃ  srūtā panna satyaṃ  sakṛdā gami satyaṃ  anāgā misa tyaṃ  yāva samya ksaṃ buddhasatyaṃ  etyena satyena  satya vaca nena  śriya mahā śriye  sarva śriye  sarvā bhyo daya śriye  sarva śriya karaṇi  sarva satva hitāṃ veṣaṇi  loka dhatri śriye  śriyā pari vṛ te  ava tara utama karaṇi śriye  devi devate māṃ prekṣya rakṣa māṃ  sarva bhaye bhyaḥ  sarvo padrave bhyaḥ  sarva vyā dhi bhyaḥ  sarva jana ñcameva śamā naya  sarva arthā ñcame sādhaya  ida ñcame kārya ṅkuru  namaḥ śuddhavāse bhyo  bodhi satve bhyaḥ  śakke  taṭe taṭe  kaṭe kuṭe  karaṭe kaṅkaṭe  karoṭi  aśrā nte vighoṇi  svāhā  karoṭi nīye  svāhā  kampi nīye  svāhā  kampi nīye  svāhā  ciri miri ṇiye  svāhā  namaḥ parama śuddhacittānāṃ  bodhi satvānāṃ  siddhyantume mantra padā  svāhā

namo phai ṣajya guru vaiḍū rya prabha sya  tathā gata sya rha taḥ samya ksaṃ buddhasya  namo buddhasya  namo dharmma sya  namo saṅgha sya  namo amitā bhaya tathā gatāya rhate samya ksaṃ buddhāya  namaḥ āryā valokite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  namaḥ ārya mahā sthāma praptaya  bodhi satvāya  namaḥ sarva artha siddhaya vidyā dhara rājāya  namo mahā śriyāye sarva artha sādhī kāye  tadyathā  deva satyaṃ  indra satyaṃ  brahma satyaṃ  iṛṣi satyaṃ  saṃ vṛ tisa tyaṃ  paramā rtha satyaṃ  śrāva kasa tyaṃ  duḥ kha satyaṃ  samu daya satyaṃ  niru dhasatyaṃ  mārga satyaṃ  anā gāmi satyaṃ  arha satyaṃ  pratyeka buddhasatyaṃ  bodhi satva satyaṃ  upa ryu pari satyānaṃ  samya ksaṃ buddhasatyaṃ  etena satyena  satya vaca nena  śriye mahā śriye  sarvā bhyo daya śriye  ava tara utama karaṇī śriye  devate māṃ prekṣa rakṣa rakṣa māṃ  sarva bhaye bhyaḥ  sarva arthāṃ me sādhaya  namaḥ śuddhā vāsānāṃ bodhi satvānāṃ  ebhyo nama skṛtvā  imāṃ vidyāṃ prava kṣyā mi  same vidyā sa mṛddhya tu  tadyathā  śakke śakaṭe  kuṭe karaṭe  ka ṅkaṭe  kara ṅkaṭe  karoṭi nīye  svāhā  vimi nīye  svāhā  viloki nīye  svāhā  yaśāya  svāhā  yaśavatīye  svāhā  yaśo dharāya  svāhā  śubhaya  svāhā  śubhavatīye  svāhā  rūpāya  svāhā  rūpa vatīye  svāhā  suva rṇṇāya  svāhā  suva rṇṇa suva rṇṇāya  svāhā  padma vatīye  svāhā  mahā śriye  svāhā

20、卍不思议观陀罗尼真言卍 不思议观陀罗尼真言品第二十二

nama strya dhva nugata  prati ṣṭhite bhyaḥ  sarva tathā gate bhyaḥ  mahā bodhi satva gaṇa vare bhyaḥ  namaḥ ārya vajra dhara  sarva maṇḍala devata vidyā rāje bhyaḥ  oṃ  amoghā valokita  mahā maṇḍala padme  sarva bodhi satva nama skṛte  bhara bhara  samantā valokite  amogha mahā brahma veṣa dhara  dhara dhara  mahā kāru ṇikā  bodhaya bodhaya  mahā bodhini  padma bodhini  sarva papā ndhakara  praśamani  sarva durgati varaka  mahā kāru ṇika  bahu vivi dhaveṣa dhara  sarva tathā gata garbha  huru huru  amogha garbhe  turu turu  amogha paśahaste  muru muru  vimo kṣa  bhuje  kṣiṇi kṣiṇi  sarva ava raṇa viśuddhe  bhara bhara  sarva tathā gata paripu rate  tara tara  tāraya māṃ  ava lokaya  padma bhuje  maṇi kanaka  vibhu ṣita bahu  dama dama  durda ntanāṃ  mahā bodhi satva varada  mahā kāru ṇika  sarva devata nama skṛta  iṛṣi gaṇa sata mita  śata saha sra  candra sūrya treka  raśmi rava bha sita  mahā paśu pati veṣa dhara  parama śuddha satva  avalokite śvara  mahe śvara  parama kāru ṇika  mahā maṇḍale śvara  supra buddha mahā padma bhuje śvara  mahā vidyā dhare śvara  dhiri dhiri  mahā dhiri  mahā kāru ṇika  mahā vimo kṣa maṇḍala dhara  sarva tathā gata guhya  mudra samaya dhara  mahā bala vīrya dhara  maṇi moli dhara  amitā bhama kuṭa dhara  dhuru dhuru  samantā valokita  loke śvara  paśa dhare śvara  para para  mahā maitrī vilokita  sarva satva sa nta raka  siddhya siddhya  śapa ripū raka  mahā bala prada  namo stute  svāhā  oṃ  dhira dhira  mahā maṇḍala viśva rūpa  ṣa ṭpara mita pari puraka  sarva bodhi satva nama skṛta  parama vipula vimo kṣa dhara  mahā paśa vilokita  amogha paśa jvalita  mahā jvalā valokita  mahā maṇi dīpta dhara  samanta vabha sita  jvala jvala  mahā ga mbhī ra vimo kṣa paśa dhara  bala bodhi ṅga pāka rṣaka  oṃ  brahma rūpa  mahā mogha paśa hūṃ hūṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  sarva satvā valokita  vara prada  namo stute  svāhā

44、卍不空大可畏明王央俱舍真言(不空大可畏明王央俱舍陀罗尼)卍
nama strya dhva nugata prati ṣṭhite bhyaḥ  namaḥ sarva tathā gate bhyo  namaḥ sarva buddha bodhi satva  ārya vajra dhara mahā maṇḍala devate bhyaḥ  namaḥ sarva pratyeka buddhā  rya śravaka saṅghe bhyo 卍清净莲华明王央俱舍真言(清净莲花明王央俱舍陀罗尼)卍
nama strya dhva nugata  prati ṣṭhite bhyaḥ  sarva buddha bodhi satva  prasara tathā gata guhya  maṇḍala mudrā mantra  prasara samu dre bhyaḥ  namaḥ ārya vajra dhara  sarva kula guhya vidyā dhari ndra prati ṣṭhite bhyaḥ  namaḥ sarva pratyeka buddhā rya śrā vaka saṅghe bhyo  tīta nagata pratyu tpanne bhyaḥ  namaḥ sarva maṇḍala guhya  mahā vidyā rāja sadhana siddhe bhyaḥ  namo ratna trayāya  namaḥ āryā valo kite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  mahā kāru ṇikāya  sarva vidyā maṇḍala rāja  mahā mogha vikurvaṇa siddhe bhyaḥ  sarva mudre bhyaḥ  tadyathā  oṃ  vimale  vimala garbhe  vimalāṃ muja padme  surya varcase  saha sra raśmi kiraṇe  mahā raśmi jvalā vabha site  cara cara  cacara  sañcara  padmo tari  padma garbhe  padma bhuje  suni rmalaṃ muja vimale  maṇi kanaka  vajra vai ḍuri ndra nīla mara kata  padma rāga  vivi dhamahā maṇi  ratnālaṅkṛta śarire  dhara dhara  mahā padma dhare  para para  paraśu paśadhare  sara sara  samanta vairo cana  sarva tathā gata guhyā dhiṣṭhite  kula samayaṃ  pari pūraṇi  dhara dhara  vajra jvalā māla garbhe  vajra vajre  vajrā dhiṣṭhita padme  hūṃ hūṃ  maṇi maṇi  mahā maṇi  cinta maṇi paśadhara  huru huru  padme padme gaure  padma paṇi varade  amogha padme  oṃ  padmini  padma maṇi vajra dhare  sarva tathā gata kula sāmā nya  samayā dhiṣṭhite  mahā vipula bhuje  bhara bhara  saṃ bhara saṃ bhara  bhuru bhuru  bhu raṇi  bhiri bhiri  samantā valokita vidyā rāje  prasara prasara  samanta vimale  sarva vidyā maṇḍala devata  nama skṛte  tara tara  tāraya tāraya  samantāśā pari pūraṇi  sarva bodhi satvā bhiṣe cani  sarva tathā gatā moghā bhiṣikte  abhiṣi ñcaya māṃ  sarva vidyā maṇḍala  kula samayā bhiṣekeḥ  sarva tathā gata pāṇi varade  padma gauri  padma prabhe  padma vikajaṃ muja garbhe  hūṃ hūṃ  vajre vajre  vajra padme  tathā gata kulā dhiṣṭhite  amogha varade  sarvā śāpari pūraṇi  sarvā pāya duḥ kha praśamani  amogha hṛdaya siddhi  sādhaya vimale  hūṃ  phaṭ  oṃ  varade padma bhuje  namo stute  padma puṭe  svāhā

sunaya gate  avila vivarjiti  madha vivarjite
mana vivarjite  hata vivarjite  hanaya vivarjite
gana vivarjite  kala vivarjite  asala vivarjite
naya gate  dhṛti gate  mati gate  smṛti gate
tathā gata gate
asanrevedānugate
dharmma dhātu asa nrevedā nugate gate  vinaya gate
sarva veda vajra maya samādhi mukha gate
sarva tathā gata mukha naya
yāvanu buddha tryadhva samanta guṇa śasa
tathā gata bhūme  anu buddhā nugate  svāhā

八、卍一切如来心秘密全身舍利宝箧印陀罗尼卍（一遍）
nama strya dhvikānāṃ
sarva tathā gatānāṃ  oṃ  bhuvi bhava navare  vacare  cacaṭe culu culu  dhara dhara
sarva tathā gatā dhātū dhāre  padmāṃ bhavati  jaya vare  mucule   smara  tathā gata dharmma cakra  pravarttana vajre  bodhi maṇḍā laṅkārā  laṅkṛte
sarva tathā gatā dhiṣṭhite  bodhaya bodhaya  bodhi bodhi  buddhya buddhya  saṃbodhani  saṃbodhaya  cala cala calantu  sarvā vara ṇani  sarva papa vigate  huru huru  sarva śoka vigate
sarva tathā gata hṛdaya vajreṇi  saṃbhara saṃbhara
sarva tathā gata guhya dhāraṇi mudre  buddhe subuddhe
sarva tathā gatā dhiṣṭhite dhātū garbhe  svāhā  samayā dhiṣṭhite svāhā
sarva tathā gata hṛdaya dhātu mudre  svāhā  supratiṣṭhita stūpe  tathā gatā dhiṣṭhite  huru huru  hūṃ hūṃ  svāhā  oṃ
sarva tathā gata uṣṇīṣa  dhātu mudrāṇi
sarva tathā gatāṃ  sadhātū vibhuṣitā dhiṣṭhite  hūṃ hūṃ  svāhā

九、卍一切诸佛心印陀罗尼卍（一遍）
tadyathā   hara hara  cala cala  sañcala  sañcala  tala tala  santala  santala  hinī  riṇī  samariṇī  ranapati  ranapati  lokadhāri  lokadhāri  loka dhāṇi  loka dhāriṇi  vara vara  phula phula  vāra vāra  mahā vijayā  vahitī  hana hana  sarva buddha pirī ṣitī  sarva padhīsanā  aparācitī  pratibhāna sapadī  satvā valokitī  sarva buddha prati maṇitī  bhagavati  sara sara   prasara  prasara  visara  visara  sarva doṣā  pagatī  svāhā

十一、卍法供养十方三世一切如来真言(回向陀罗尼)卍（七遍）
oṃ   smara  smara  vimāna  sāra  mahajakra  va  hūṃ
